chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg:CREATE PROGRAM  CHS_DC_MEDORDERS_OPS : DBA
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg:SET  TOTAL_ORDERS  =  0
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg:( ORDERS  O ),
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg: ENC [ EC ]-> ORD [ OC ]-> LAST_ACTION_SEQUENCE =O.LAST_ACTION_SEQUENCE, TOTAL_ORDERS =(
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg: TOTAL_ORDERS + 1 ),
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg:SET  ORDERSPERSECOND  =  22
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg:SET  ESTTIME  =  TOTAL_ORDERS / ORDERSPERSECOND / 60
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg: CALL ECHO ( BUILD ( "*     Active Orders = " ,  TOTAL_ORDERS ))
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg: CALL ECHO ( BUILD2 ( "Cleaning " ,  TOTAL_ORDERS ,  " active orders" ))
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg:UPDATE FROM ( ORDERS  O ) SET O.ORDER_STATUS_CD= OSTATUS -> COMPLETED_CD ,
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg:UPDATE FROM ( ORDERS  O ) SET O.ORDER_STATUS_CD= OSTATUS -> DISCONTINUED_CD ,
chs_dc_medorder_ops.prg: CALL ECHO ( BUILD2 ( TOTAL_ORDERS ,  " orders have been cleaned" ))
